***стать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>стать</a> (11761)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ти</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stand, become</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*steh₂-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stand</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>стать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">statʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:становиться.html>станови́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stand in a certain location or near someone or something (interchangeable with <a href = vnd.unilang:встать.html>встать</a>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>Ста́нь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:потеряться.html>потеря́ешься</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Stanʹ</b> ko mne, a to poterjáješʹsja.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Stand near me so you don't get lost.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>Ста́нь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мно́ю</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:потеряться.html>потеря́ешься</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Stanʹ</b> so mnóju, a to poterjáješʹsja.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Stand near me so you don't get lost.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ньте</a></b> побли́же.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Stánʹte</b> poblíže.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Get closer.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ньте</a></b> лу́чше <a href = vnd.unilang:сюда.html>сюда́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вдруг.html>вдруг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сосулька.html>сосу́льки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:упасть.html>упаду́т</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Stánʹte</b> lúčše sjudá, a to vdrug sosúlʹki upadút.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Better stand here in case icicles suddenly fall.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ньте</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очередь.html>о́чередь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:молодой.html>молодо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́к</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>Вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:долго.html>до́лго</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:очередь.html>о́череди</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дете</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:потерпеть.html>потерпи́те</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Stánʹte</b> v óčeredʹ, molodój čelovék! Vy ne dólgo v óčeredi že búdete stojátʹ, poterpíte.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Stand in the queue, young man! You won't be standing in the queue for long, have some patience.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with imperfective infinitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to begin to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́нут</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гонять.html>гоня́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крыса.html>кры́с</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Stánut</b> li gonjátʹ oní krýs?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Will</b> they <b>start</b> chasing the rats?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with imperfective infinitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come to pass
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:писать.html>писа́ть</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>stal</b> pisátʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b>began</b> to write.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with imperfective infinitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take to
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пить.html>пить</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>stal</b> pitʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b>took</b> to drinking.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in negative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with imperfective infinitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be not going to; <span class="use-with-mention">used to express a determined negative attitude</span>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1887</b>,  Антон Павлович <a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>Че́хов</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Pavlovich Chekhov</a>), Constance Garnett, transl., <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%94%D0%B0%D1%87%D0%BD%D0%B8%D0%BA%D0%B8_(%D0%A7%D0%B5%D1%85%D0%BE%D0%B2)" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Дачники (Чехов)">«<a href = vnd.unilang:темнота.html>Темнота́</a>»</a></cite>  | <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Darkness_(Chekhov/Garnett)" class="extiw" title="s:Darkness (Chekhov/Garnett)">Darkness</a></cite> | :</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">— <a href = vnd.unilang:ваш.html>ва́ше</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:благородие.html>благоро́дие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:опять.html>опя́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:твой.html>твое́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:милость.html>ми́лости</a>! — <a href = vnd.unilang:начать.html>на́чал</a> кири́ла. — <a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>Вот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>отцо́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>пришёл</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:сделать.html>сде́лай</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:милость.html>ми́лость</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:отпустить.html>отпусти́</a> ва́ську! <a href = vnd.unilang:непременный.html>непреме́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:член.html>член</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разговаривать.html>разгова́ривать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́л</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́т</a>: «<a href = vnd.unilang:пойти.html>Пошёл</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вон.html>вон</a>!»</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">— Váše blagoródije, ja opjátʹ k tvojéj mílosti! — náčal Kiríla. — Vot s otcóm prišól, sdélaj mílostʹ, otpustí Vásʹku! Nepreménnyj člen razgovárivatʹ <b>ne stal</b>. Govorít: “Pošól <a href = vnd.unilang:вон.html>von</a>!”</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">"Your honour, I have come again to ask your gracious mercy," began Kirila. "Here I have come with my father. Be merciful, let Vaska go! The permanent member <b>would not</b> talk to me. He said: 'Go away!'"</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стан.html>ста́ну</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:делать.html>де́лать</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja ne <b>stánu</b> étovo délatʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’m not going to do it.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> in negative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pass away
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ло</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jevó ne <b>stálo</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He has passed away.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to at all costs
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ло</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vo što by to ni <b>stálo</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">at all costs</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to therefore
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>быть</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stálo</b> bytʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">therefore; consequently; and so</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with instrumental case<span class="ib-comma">,</span> impersonal with dative case</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become, to get, to grow
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:летчик.html>лётчиком</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>stal</b> ljótčikom.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He became a pilot.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:седой.html>седы́м</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>stal</b> sedým.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He became grey-haired.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:учитель.html>учи́телем</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>stal</b> učítelem.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I became a teacher.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>Всем</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скучно.html>ску́чно</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vsem <b>stálo</b> skúšno/skúčno.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Everyone was bored.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>стать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">statʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:статья.html>ста́тей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>build</li>
<li>trait, character, type
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>стать</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oná jemú pod <b>statʹ</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She is a match for him.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>need
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>С</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ти</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">S kakój <b>státi</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(<i>colloquial</i>) Why should I/you/he/she/it/we/they? For what reason?; why?</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***статься.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:статься.html>ста́ться</a> (15093)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стать.html>ста́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">státʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:статься.html>ста́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">státʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to become, to happen
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:статься.html>ста́лось</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">što s nim <b>stálosʹ</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what has become of him?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:статься.html>ста́ться</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">móžet <b>státʹsja</b>, što</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it may happen that</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:вполне.html>вполне́</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:статься.html>ста́ться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">(vpolné) móžet <b>státʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">it is (quite) possible/probable</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебя́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:статься.html>ста́нется</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s tebjá <b>stánetsja</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one can well expect that from you!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***стационарный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стационарный.html>стациона́рный</a> (13618)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">statiōnārius</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. In the meaning "hospital (relational)", from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стационар.html>стациона́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stacionár</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стационарный.html>стациона́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stacionárnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>stationary, fixed, permanent
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стационарный.html>стациона́рная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:антенна.html>анте́нна</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stacionárnaja</b> antɛ́nna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">fixed antenna</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стационарный.html>стациона́рная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:библиотека.html>библиоте́ка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stacionárnaja</b> bibliotéka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">permanent library</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hospital
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стационарный.html>стациона́рный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stacionárnyj</b> bolʹnój</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in-patient; hospital patient</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стачка.html>ста́чка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stáčka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стачка.html>ста́чки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стачка.html>ста́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стачк</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>strike
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:всеобщий.html>всео́бщая</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стачка.html>ста́чка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vseóbščaja <b>stáčka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">general strike</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:политический.html>полити́ческая</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:экономический.html>экономи́ческая</a>) <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стачка.html>ста́чка</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">politíčeskaja (ekonomíčeskaja) <b>stáčka</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">political (economic) strike</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устраивать.html>устра́ивать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стачка.html>ста́чку</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ustráivatʹ <b>stáčku</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to strike; go on strike</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:руководить.html>руководи́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стачка.html>ста́чкой</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rukovodítʹ <b>stáčkoj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to conduct a strike</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свобода.html>свобо́да</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стачка.html>ста́чек</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">svobóda <b>stáček</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">freedom to strike</span></div></dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стащить.html>стащи́ть</a> (6567)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>тащи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">taščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стащить.html>стащи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">staščítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стаскивать.html>ста́скивать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>тащи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drag off, to drag down, to pull off, to pull down
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стаскивать.html>ста́скивать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stáskivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to drag into, to pull into
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стаскивать.html>ста́скивать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stáskivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to steal, to filch, to pinch, to swipe
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тащить.html>тащи́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">taščítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стая.html>ста́я</a> (4911)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">стаꙗ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">staja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cattleshed, shelter, tent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stьvolъ</i>.

***створка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:створка.html>ство́рка</a> (9415)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">створи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stvorítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:створка.html>ство́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stvórka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:створка.html>ство́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:створка.html>ство́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:створка.html>ство́рок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">architecture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> leaf, fold, panel (One of the movably attached, opening and closing parts or halves of a structure, gate, window, etc. Each of the components of a portable folding mirror, screen, etc.)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">одноство́рчатый</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">odnostvórčatyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стегать.html>стега́ть</a> (26594)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стегать.html>стега́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stegátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стегнуть.html>стегну́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стегану́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to whip, to lash, to flog</li></ol>

***стегнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стегнуть.html>стегну́ть</a> (30395)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стегать.html>стега́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stegátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стегнуть.html>стегну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stegnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стегать.html>стега́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to whip, to lash, to flog <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">once</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стегану́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">steganútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стезя.html>стезя́</a> (21629)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">стьзꙗ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stĭzja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stьdza</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">path</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*stigaˀ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*stigʰ-eh₂</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стезя.html>стезя́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stezjá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стезя.html>стези́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стезя.html>стези́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стезя.html>стезе́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> path, way</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стек.html>стек</a> (25747)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_2">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stick</i>.

</p>
<ol><li>riding crop</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">stecca</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стек.html>сте́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stɛ́ka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стек.html>сте́ки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стек.html>сте́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стек.html>стек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sculpting</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> modeling tool <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">wooden, bone or metal tool for sculpting clay or similar soft material, with a wide, blade-like end</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стекать.html>стека́ть</a> (7579)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сте́к-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sték-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стекать.html>стека́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stekátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стечь</b>)

***стекло.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стекло.html>стекло́</a> (790)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stьklo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gothic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Gothic language">Gothic</a></span> <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐍃𐍄𐌹𐌺𐌻𐍃</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stikls</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:склянка.html>скля́нка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skljánka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">phial; bottle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*steyg-</i>, whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stick</i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">sklo</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стекло.html>стекло́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stekló</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стекло.html>стекла́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стекло.html>стёкла</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стекло.html>стёкол</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>glass</li>
<li>chimney (of kerosene lamp)</li>
<li>pane, window, lens</li></ol>

***стеклянный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стеклянный.html>стекля́нный</a> (2624)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">стьклѧнꙑи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stĭklęnyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stьklo, *-ěnъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стеклянный.html>стекля́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stekljánnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>glass, glassy, vitreous</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стелить.html>стели́ть</a> (22565)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stьlati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to spread</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*stel-</i> / <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*stl-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стелить.html>стели́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stelítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постелить.html>постели́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to spread, to lay, to make <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">bed</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мама.html>ма́ма</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стелить.html>сте́лет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:постель.html>посте́ль</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Máma <b>stélet</b> mne postélʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Mum is making a bed for me.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дем</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стелить.html>стели́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:линолеум.html>лино́леум</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kogdá búdem <b>stelítʹ</b> linóleum?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">When shall we put linoleum on?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мягкий.html>мя́гко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стелить.html>сте́лет</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жесткий.html>жёстко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спать.html>спать</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">proverb</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mjáxko stélet, da žóstko spatʹ</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">iron fist in velvet glove, a honey tongue, a heart of gall</span></dd><dd>(literally, “<span class="e-literally">he makes a soft bed but it's hard to sleep on it</span>”)</dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стлать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stlatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:застилать.html>застила́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zastilátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***стелиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стелиться.html>стели́ться</a> (25540)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стелить.html>стели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стелиться.html>стели́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stelítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to spread, to spread out, to sprawl</li>
<li>to lie on the ground</li>
<li>to creep <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a plant</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to speed over a surface <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of animals and birds</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to prepare for bed
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">постлели́ться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">postlelítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стелить.html>стели́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stelítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
